add_namespace = newengland

### Creating New England
country_event = { # Occupy New England
	id = newengland.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.1"}
	title = newengland.1.t
	desc = newengland.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = newengland.1.a
		ai_chance = { # Take New England
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_TAKE
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = USA
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					tag = USA
					tag = CSA
					tag = TEX
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { NFL = { country_event = nfl_flavour.1 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_TAKE
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.2290
				days = 130
				random_days = 130
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # ACW nation informed that Canada has seized New England
	id = newengland.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.2"}
	title = newengland.2.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots
	
	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d
		trigger = { country_exists = CSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d.nocsa
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = CSA } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = occupied_new_england
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # This means War!
		name = newengland.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = USA
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
					NOT = { country_exists = TEX }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = TEX
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CAN
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = { # Next time Canada!
		name = newengland.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada doesn't occupy New England
	id = newengland.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.3"}
	title = newengland.3.t
	desc = newengland.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_england_units
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = USA_civil_war_newengland
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada Releases New England
	id = newengland.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.5"}
	title = newengland.5.t
	desc = newengland.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		is_faction_leader = yes
		932 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
			} #Massachusetts
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = CSA
			country_exists = NEE
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_CAN_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_WASHINGTON_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_KENNEDY_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_ASTOR_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_MILITARY_COUP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_LOVECRAFT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.101
					days = 9
				}
				country_event = {
					id = miscnee.153
					days = 245
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.5.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.101
					days = 9
				}
				country_event = {
					id = miscnee.153
					days = 245
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			change_tag_from = CAN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_state
		set_country_flag = CAN_new_england_decision
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				CAN_yankee_rebellion = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance"	}
				CAN = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { CAN USA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.5.e
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				set_country_flag = NEE_Gov_Gen
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			change_tag_from = CAN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.5.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			 modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_DEMOCRAT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_LIBERAL_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_NATIONAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_FEDERALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_REMNANT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_SENTINEL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_STODDARD
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_QUAKER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_PROHIBITION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_RADSOC
					}	
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_START_PATH_SYNDIE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				set_country_flag = NEE_Gov_Gen
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # America is reunited
	id = newengland.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.7"}
	title = newengland.7.t
	desc = newengland.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		owns_state = 361 #Maryland
		owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
		owns_state = 395 #Illinois
		owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
		owns_state = 365 #Georgia
		OR = {
			owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
			has_global_flag = CAL_seperatist_claim
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_united_america
			has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_BCC
			has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_nordic_united
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = COR
			has_war_with = CAL
			AND = {
				country_exists = TXS
				has_country_flag = TXS_claimed_america
				is_ally_of_ROOT = no
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = NYC
				has_country_flag = NYC_can_invade_america
				is_ally_of_ROOT = no
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = BBR
				has_country_flag = BBR_claimed_america
				is_ally_of_ROOT = no
			}
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = { 
					has_country_flag = NEE_lovecraftians_win
					has_country_flag = NEE_lovecraft_lives
				}
			}
		}
		name = newengland.7.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
		set_country_flag = NEE_united_america
		if = {
			limit = {
			   NOT = {
				OR = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_nordic_league_tag_national_populist
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_radical_america_national_populist
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_national_populist_ancap
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_paternal_autocrat_ancap
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_LERMOND_FLAG
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ECOANARCHISM
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_FOSTERAULT
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_HIVE
				has_country_flag = NEE_kingdom
				has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_new_ireland
				has_completed_focus = NEE_New_Sons_of_Liberty
				has_completed_focus = NEE_prohibition_victory
				has_completed_focus = NEE_quakervictory
				}
			   }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_LERMOND_FLAG
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_nordic_league_tag_national_populist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_nordic_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_radical_america_national_populist
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_paternal_autocrat_ancap
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_national_populist_ancap
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ancap_USA
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = newenglandmilflavor.1004
					days = 20
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ECOANARCHISM
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ECOANARCHISM_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_FOSTERAULT
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_FOSTERAULT_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_HIVE
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_HIVE_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_new_ireland
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america_new_ireland
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			    has_completed_focus = NEE_quakervictory
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_quaker_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			   has_completed_focus = NEE_prohibition_victory
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_prohib_america
			country_event = {
				id = miscnee.203
				days = 5
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = miscnee.204
				    days = 20
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Groves_Commands_our_Armies
			}
			complete_national_focus = NEE_National_Healing
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_GROVES_COMMONWEALTH
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_war_aftermath_idea
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_political_aftermath_idea
			set_country_flag = NEE_groves_post
			hidden_effect = {
				create_corps_commander = {
				name = "William C. Westmoreland"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_William_Westmoreland_general.png"
				traits = { infantry_officer }
				skill = 2

				attack_skill = 2
				defense_skill = 1
				planning_skill = 3
				logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Pershing_Guides_our_Sons
			}
			complete_national_focus = NEE_National_Healing
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_pershing_snake_america
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_war_aftermath_idea
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_political_aftermath_idea
			set_country_flag = NEE_pershing_post
			hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newenglandmilflavor.1002 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = newenglandmilflavor.1003 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Bingham_Protects_our_People
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_bingham_convetion
				}
			}
			complete_national_focus = NEE_National_Healing
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_war_aftermath_idea
			add_ideas = USA_civil_war_political_aftermath_idea
			set_country_flag = NEE_bingham_post
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.3016 days = 15 random_days = 45 } #Leave Entente?
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = miscnee.176 days = 35 }
			country_event = { id = miscnee.180 days = 35 }
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = { id = worldnews.44 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_template = "Resistance"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Resistance"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_ACW_cores = yes
			}
			if = {
				 limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = NEE_New_Sons_of_Liberty
					}
				 }
				 country_event = {
				id = miscnee.185
				days = 3
			}
			}
			if = {
				 limit = {

					has_completed_focus = NEE_New_Sons_of_Liberty

				 }
				 country_event = {
				id = miscnee.1855
				days = 3
			}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				country_event = { id = miscnee.1 days = 600 random_days = 200 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_country_flag = NEE_lovecraftians_win
				has_country_flag = NEE_lovecraft_lives
			}
		}
		name = newengland.7.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
		set_country_flag = NEE_united_america
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america_lovecraft
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_template = "Resistance"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Resistance"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_ACW_cores = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Labor-Relations act(worker friendly)
	id = newengland.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.10"}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # don't Pass the Act
		name = newengland.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_ideas = NEE_labor_relations1
		add_political_power = -80
	}
	option = { # don't Pass the Act
		name = newengland.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_political_power = 80
	}
}

country_event = { # New England requests home rule
	id = newengland.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.12"}
	title = newengland.12.t
	desc = newengland.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NEE = {
			is_subject_of = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {

### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1944 National Party Primary
	id = newengland.2525
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.25"}
	title = newengland.2525.t
	desc = { # National Party has the Presidency
		text = newengland.2525.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # National Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.2525.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Frances Perkins
		name = newengland.2525.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_perkins
		}
	}
	option = { # Ernest W. Gibson
		name = newengland.2525.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_gibson
		}
	}
	option = { # Aiken
		name = newengland.2525.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_aiken
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.2525.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = { has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea }
		}
	}
}

			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.27.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Christian Herter
		name = newengland.27.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_democratic_primary_herter
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = newengland.27.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}
}

				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edmund_Baker_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sde
			}
			if = { # Colvin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_colvin
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_David_Leigh_Colvin_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edmund_Baker_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sde
				
			}
			if = { # Watson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_watson
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edmund_Baker_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sde
			}
			if = { # Upshaw
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_upshaw
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_William_D_Upshaw_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edmund_Baker_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sde
			}
			if = { # Shuler
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_shuler
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_Robert_P_Shuler_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edmund_Baker_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Roger_Babson_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sde
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			
			if = { # Roger Babson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_babson
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Roger Babson"
					desc = "POLITICS_ROGER_BABSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Roger_Babson.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_humanistic_capitalism_subtype
					traits = {
						economic_reformer
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Claude A Watson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_watson
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Claude A. Watson"
					desc = "POLITICS_CLAUDE_WATSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Claude_Watson.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_christian_socialism_subtype
					traits = {
						staunch_prohibitionist
					}
				}
			}

			if = { # William Upshaw
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_upshaw
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "William D. Upshaw"
					desc = "POLITICS_ROBERT_SHULER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_William_D_Upshaw.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = popular_patriotism_subtype
					traits = {
						economic_reformer
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Robert Shuler
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1944_prohibition_primary_shuler
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Robert P. Shuler"
					desc = "POLITICS_ROBERT_SHULER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Robert_P_Shuler.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_progressive_conservatism_subtype
					traits = { staunch_prohibitionist }
				}
			}
		}
	}

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###

country_event = { # 1948 National Party Primary
	id = newengland.2929
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.29"}
	title = newengland.2929.t
	desc = { # National Party has the Presidency
		text = newengland.2929.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # National Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.2929.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Frances Perkins
		name = newengland.2929.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_perkins
		}
	}
	option = { # Ernest W. Gibson
		name = newengland.2929.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_gibson
		}
	}
	option = { # Aiken
		name = newengland.2929.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_aiken
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.2929.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = { has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1948 election
	id = newengland.32
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.32"}
	title = newengland.32.t
	desc = newengland.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Eleanor Roosevelt
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_quaker_primary_roosevelt
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Eleanor Roosevelt"
					desc = "POLITICS_ELANOR_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Eleanor_Roosevelt.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = quaker_socialism_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_first_lady_of_the_revolution
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Clarence Pickett
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_quaker_primary_pickett
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Clarence Pickett"
					desc = "POLITICS_CLARENCE_PICKETT_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Clarence_Pickett.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = quaker_socialism_subtype
					traits = { determined_peacemaker }
				}
			}
			if = { # Wilson A. Head
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_quaker_primary_head
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Wilson A. Head"
					desc = "POLITICS_WILSON_HEAD_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Wilson_Head.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = quaker_socialism_subtype
					traits = {
						race_relation_pioneer
					}

			}
			if = { # Jean Toomer

				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Jean Toomer"
					desc = "POLITICS_JEAN_TOOMER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Jean_Toomer.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = quaker_socialism_subtype
					traits = {
						popular_author
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Maurice J. Tobin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_republican_primary_tobin
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Maurice J. Tobin"
					desc = "POLITICS_MAURICE_TOBIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Maurice_Tobin.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = centrist_subtype
					traits = { NEE_friend_of_labour }
				}
			}
			if = { # Paul A. Dever
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_republican_primary_dever
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Paul A. Dever"
					desc = "POLITICS_PAUL_DEVER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Paul_A_Dever.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = centrist_subtype
					traits = { armaments_organizer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Paul A. Dever
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_republican_primary_bowles
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Chester B. Bowles"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHESTER_BOWLES_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Chester_Bowles.png"

					ideology = centrist_subtype
					traits = { NEE_foreign_aid_proponent }
				}
			}

				limit = {

				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Robert F. Bradford"

					traits = { economist }
				}
			}
			if = { # Thomas C. Hart
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_democrat_primary_hart
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thomas C. Hart"
					desc = "POLITICS_THOMAS_HART_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Thomas_Hart.png"

					traits = { quartermaster_general }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Progressive
		name = newengland.24.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1948_election_liberal
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prohbs_in_power
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = NEE_social_democrat_party
				long_name = NEE_social_democrat_party_long
				ideology = social_democrat
			}
			clr_country_flag = prohbs_in_power
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.3434
				days = 1265
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.3426
				days = 1276
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.34
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.35
				days = 1289
			}
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.36
				days = 1295
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Frances Perkins
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_perkins
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frances Perkins"
					desc = "POLITICS_FRANCES_PERKINS_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Frances_Perkins.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = liberal_socialism_subtype
					traits = {
						economic_reformer
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = NEE_Frances_Perkins_hog_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Frederick_Hale_for_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Scott_Nearing_eco_sde
				add_ideas = NEE_Edith_Nourse_Rogers_sec_sde
				
			}
			if = { # George Aiken
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_1948_liberal_primary_aiken
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Aiken"
					desc = "POLITICS_GEORGE_AIKEN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_George_Aiken.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_jeffersonianism_subtype
					traits = {
						NEE_defender_of_the_common_folk
					}
				}

### 1952 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1952 National Party Primary
	id = newengland.3434
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.34"}
	title = newengland.3434.t
	desc = { # National Party has the Presidency
		text = newengland.1952.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # National Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.1952.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Frances Perkins
		name = newengland.3434.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_liberal_primary_perkins
		}
	}
	option = { # Ernest W. Gibson
		name = newengland.3434.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_liberal_primary_gibson
		}
	}
	option = { # Aiken
		name = newengland.3434.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1944_liberal_primary_aiken
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.3434.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = { has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1952 Quaker Party Primary
	id = newengland.3426
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.34"}
	title = newengland.3434.t
	desc = { # Quaker Party has the Presidency
		text = newengland.3426.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
	desc = { # Quaker Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.3426.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Clarence Pickett
		name = newengland.3426.a

			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_quaker_primary_pickett
		}
	}

		name = newengland.3426.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_quaker_primary_roosevelt

	option = { # Wilson A. Head
		name = newengland.3426.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_quaker_primary_head
		}
	}
	option = { # Bayard Rustin
		name = newengland.3426.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			NOT = { country_exists = BBR }
			NOT = { NYC = { has_country_leader = { name = "Bayard Rustin" ruling_only = yes } } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_quaker_primary_rustin
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.3426.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
}

	title = newengland.35.t
	desc = { # Republican Party won the presidency just last time
		text = newengland.35.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party does not have the Presidency
		text = newengland.35.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat 
				has_government = paternal_autocrat 
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NEE_Fed_Elections
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_the_remnant
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = NEE_socialist_victory
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Nelson Rockefeller
		name = newengland.35.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_republican_primary_rockefeller
		}
	}
	option = { # Henry C. Lodge Jr.
		name = newengland.35.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NEE_1952_republican_primary_lodge
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = newengland.35.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}
}

		}

		trigger = {

country_event = { # The Yankee Rebellion
	id = newengland.80
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.80"}
	title = newengland.80.t
	desc = newengland.80.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			357 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Maine
			934 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #New Hampshire
			933 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Vermont
			932 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Massachusetts
			935 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Rhode Island
			931 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Connecticut
			796 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN
				} #Upstate New York
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_state
			has_global_flag = NEE_rebelled_from_canada
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_new_england
						option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = CAN_in_rebellion
				ROOT = {
					add_to_variable = {
						var = CAN_yankee_rebellion
						value = 1
					}
				}
		}
	    }
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.80.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = NEE_rebelled_from_canada
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.101
					days = 9
				}
				country_event = {
					id = miscnee.153
					days = 245
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.80.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = NEE_rebelled_from_canada
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_acw_new_england
					option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		CAN_release_NEE = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				set_country_flag = NEE_Gov_Gen
			}
		}
	}
}

### Rejoining the ACW Winner
country_event = { # New England receives request
	id = newengland.90
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.90"}
	title = newengland.90.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.forced
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = NEE_legitimacy
				value = NEE_threshold
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.choice
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = NEE_legitimacy
				value = NEE_threshold
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = requester
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = NEE_threshold
				value = 40
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_threshold
					value = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.90.a #It seems we have no choice...
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.93
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.90.b #We should reunite
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = NEE_legitimacy
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = NEE_legitimacy
					value = 80
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.93
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.90.c #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.99
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # New England peacefully reuniting
	id = newengland.93
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.93"}
	title = newengland.93.t
	desc = newengland.93.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = NEE
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAN
			has_war_with = NEE
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.93.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NEE = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = NEE
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = NEE
					}
					remove_claim_by = NEE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = NEE
					}
					remove_core_of = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_nee_disobeyed
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				clr_country_flag = CAN_nee_disobeyed
				country_event = {
					id = newengland.100
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused to join
	id = newengland.99
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.99"}
	title = newengland.99.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.exists
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.notexists
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NEE
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 186
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						state = 357 #Maine
						state = 934 #New Hampshire
						state = 933 #Vermont
						state = 932 #Massachusetts
						state = 935 #Rhode Island
						state = 931 #Connecticut
						state = 796 #Upstate New York
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = newengland.99.a #Then it's war!
		trigger = {
			event_target:war_country = {
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:war_country = {
					tag = CAN
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				set_country_flag = ACW_new_england_war@ROOT
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.99.b #We'll deal with this later
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			modifier = ITA_outraged
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Democracy
	id = newengland.140
	title = newengland.140.t
	desc = newengland.140.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #The Nockian Policy
		name = newengland.140.a
		add_political_power = 45
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.4 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.4020 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = { #The Moderated Policy
		name = newengland.140.b
		add_political_power = 45
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.4 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.1 }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			long_name = NEE_ancap_market_liberal_party_long
			name = NEE_ancap_market_liberal_party 
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Albert Jay Nock"
			desc = "POLITICS_Albert_Jay_Nock_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Albert_Jay_Nock.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = libertarian_subtype
			traits = { anti_statist }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.4019 days = 7 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Tammany Hall
	id = newengland.150
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.150"}
	title = newengland.150.t
	desc = newengland.150.d
	picture = GFX_event_NEE_Tammany_Hall

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEE
		has_full_control_of_state = 358
		NOT = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
			has_government = national_populist
			OR = {
				has_war_with = CSA
				has_war_with = TEX
				has_war_with = COR
				has_war_with = USA
				has_war_with = WCC
				has_war_with = CAL
				has_war_with = BBR
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 70
	}

	option = { # Begin repairs immediately.
		name = newengland.150.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.03 }
		add_stability = 0.03
		if = {
			limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			}
			add_political_power = 30
		}
	}
}

	desc = newengland.168.d

		add_war_support = 0.10

		}

			limit = {
				COR = {
				has_war_with = USA
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			target = USA
			type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			target = WCC
			type = annex_everything
			}
			}
			if = {
			limit = {
				COR = {
				has_war_with = CSA
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			target = CSA
			type = annex_everything
			}
			}
			if = {
			limit = {
				COR = {
				has_war_with = TEX
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
			target = TEX
			type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
			limit = {
				COR = {
				has_war_with = CAL
				}

			}

			limit = {

				}
			}

			}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Stoddard makes an offer
	id = newengland.183
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.183"}
	title = newengland.183.t
	desc = newengland.183.d
	picture = GFX_CAR_klan_ballot_box

	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {  ###Offered peace###
		name = newengland.183.a
		if = {
		limit = { tag = NEE
		COR = {
		exists = yes
		has_war = no
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { tag = COR
		NEE = {
		exists = yes
		has_war = no
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.180
				days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		}
	}
	option = {  ###Finish Them###
		name = newengland.183.b
		if = {
		limit = { tag = NEE}
		declare_war_on = {
		target = COR
		type = annex_everything
		}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { tag = COR }
		declare_war_on = {
		target = NEE
		type = annex_everything
		}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NEE_start_path
						option = NEE_CAN_MONARCHY
					}

					}

			}

country_event = {# All is ready
	id = newengland.233
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.233"}
	title = newengland.233.t
	desc = newengland.233.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_bunker_hill
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			elections_allowed = no
		    }
		    add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
		    create_country_leader = {
				name = "New England Committee of Safety"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_Sons_of_Liberty.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_junta_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
			add_stability = 0.20
			add_war_support = 0.20
			remove_ideas = NEE_new_sons_resistance
			set_country_flag = NEE_REBELLION_READY
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = yes }
				overlord = {
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = KR_outraged }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				faction_leader = {
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = KR_outraged }
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = entente_research }
				remove_from_tech_sharing_group = entente_research
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea_with_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada }
				remove_ideas_with_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada
			}
			CAN_remove_from_iedc = yes
			peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_american_tag = no }
					clear_embargo_PREV = yes
				}
			}
			796 = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { is_ally_with = CAN }
					to_state = 276
				}
			}			
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CAN
				type = annex_everything
			}
			load_oob = NEE_SONS_OF_LIBERTY
			increase_conscription = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_sons_of_liberty
			set_country_flag = NEE_sons_revolt
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = newengland.233.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newenglandmilflavor.1 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = newenglandmilflavor.4 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = newenglandmilflavor.7 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.236 days = 75 }
			add_ideas = {
			NEE_Leslie_Richard_Groves_Jr_hog_ade
			NEE_Hiram_Bingham_III_for_ade
			NEE_George_Kenney_eco_pau
			NEE_George_Wesley_Griner_Jr_sec_ade
		    }
		 	if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_pissed_off_nobles
		            has_country_flag = NEE_WASHINGTON_MYTH_ACCEPTED
				}
				country_event = { id = newengland.265 days = 10 } #monarchists bois

                  country_event = { id = newengland.234 days = 10 }
                }
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #gso sad
	id = newenglandmilflavor.17
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newenglandmilflavor.9"}
	title = newenglandmilflavor.17.t
	desc = newenglandmilflavor.17.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_nova_scotia
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #og, no changes
		name = newenglandmilflavor.17.a
		add_political_power = -20
	}
	option = { #og, no changes
		name = newenglandmilflavor.17.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			overlord = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = KR_outraged }
				set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			faction_leader = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = KR_outraged }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = entente_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = entente_research
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea_with_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada
		}
		CAN_remove_from_iedc = yes
		peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = no }
				clear_embargo_PREV = yes
			}
		}
		796 = {
			teleport_armies = {
				limit = { is_ally_with = CAN }
				to_state = 276
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CAN
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #mac vists Boston, hates it and insults groves
	id = newenglandmilflavor.30
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newenglandmilflavor.9"}
	title = newenglandmilflavor.30.t
	desc = newenglandmilflavor.30.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_macarthur
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #eh
		name = newenglandmilflavor.30.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}

	option = { #that's it!
		name = newenglandmilflavor.30.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			overlord = {
				set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = entente_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = entente_research
		}
		CAN_remove_from_iedc = yes
		peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = no }
				clear_embargo_PREV = yes
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = USA
			type = annex_everything
		}
		complete_national_focus = NEE_Down_with_Macarthurs_Tyanny
		set_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = COR }
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = CAL }
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = TEX }
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = CSA }
		if = {
			limit = {
				WCC = { is_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = WCC }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TXS = { has_country_flag = TXS_claimed_america }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = TXS }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BBR = { has_country_flag = BBR_claimed_america }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = BBR }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NYC = { has_country_flag = NYC_can_invade_america }
			}
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = NYC }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				OR = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
					region = 33 #Alaska
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = NEE
		}
	}
}

		}

			bonus = 5
			uses = 5

		}

			name = csa.127.t

country_event = {# elect a monarch
	id = newengland.284
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.284"}
	title = newengland.284.t
	desc = newengland.284.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #sounds great
		name = newengland.284.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		country_event = {
			id = newengland.285
			days = 4
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = elective_monarchy_subtype
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_house_kennedy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_house_kennedy
				add_idea = NEE_elective_monarchy_idea
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_house_astor
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_house_astor
				add_idea = NEE_elective_monarchy_idea
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #nah fuck that noise
		name = newengland.284.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# elect a monarch
	id = newengland.285
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.285"}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

				days = 1460
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

			name = "Vincent, Baron Astor"

		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = NEE_Astor2_party
			long_name = NEE_Astor2_party_long
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Fish

			name = "Hamilton III, Baron Fish"
			desc = "POLITICS_HAMILTON_FISH_DESC"

		}

	option = { #Vanderbilt

				has_cosmetic_tag = ALA_LIC
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Franz Joseph II"
			desc = "POLITICS_FRANZJOSEPH_II_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ALA/Portrait_ALA_Franz_Joseph_II.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event newengland.4030"}
	title = newengland.4030.t
	desc = newengland.4030.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_military_men
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = newengland.4030.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_Chaffee_Plan
	}
	option = {
		name = newengland.4030.b
		set_country_flag = NEE_Pershing_Plan
	}
	
	option = {
		name = newengland.4030.c
		set_country_flag = NEE_Donovan_Plan
	}
	
	option = {
		name = newengland.4030.e
		set_country_flag = NEE_Grant_Plan
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event miscnee.192 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = miscnee.192.t
	desc = miscnee.192.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_petoria

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = miscnee.192.a
		add_political_power = -10
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.192.b
		trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = SPOOKY_PORTRAITS
			has_global_flag = KX_POLICEMAN_SWEAR_TO_GOD
			has_global_flag = BIDEN_VISIBLE
			has_global_flag = XINET_ON
			has_global_flag = crazy_as_fuck_poland
			has_global_flag = IMPERIUM_ON
			has_global_flag = CHRISTMAS_ON
			has_global_flag = POLAR_BEARS_ON
			has_global_flag = TROTSKY_VISIBLE
			has_global_flag = OWB_CROSSOVER_GLOBAL
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_petoria
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}

country_event = {# Alcoholics Anonymous
	id = miscnee.194
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event miscnee.194"}
	title = miscnee.194.t
	desc = miscnee.194.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_prohibs_alcoholics_anonymous
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = miscnee.194.a
		add_stability = 0.04
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_withdrawal
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NEE_withdrawal
					add_idea = NEE_withdrawal_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NEE_withdrawal_2
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = NEE_withdrawal_2
						add_idea = NEE_withdrawal_3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NEE_withdrawal_3
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = NEE_withdrawal_3
						add_idea = NEE_withdrawal_4
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NEE_withdrawal_4
					}
					remove_ideas = NEE_withdrawal_4
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_prohibition_recovery_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #Hasek-Prohibition Wargoals
	id = miscnee.210
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event miscnee.210"}
	title = miscnee.210.t
	desc = miscnee.210.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_prohibs_hasek_vs_prohibitionists

	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		OR = {
			tag = NEE
			tag = CZE
		}
		NEE = { has_idea = NEE_national_prohibition_idea }
		CZE = { has_country_leader_ideology = alcoholism_subtype }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = miscnee.210.a
		CZE = { send_embargo = NEE }
		NEE = { send_embargo = CZE }
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.210.b
		declare_war_on = {
			target = NEE
			type = annex_everything
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CZE
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Coalition Picker
	id = miscnee.212
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event miscnee.212"}
	title = miscnee.212.t
	desc = miscnee.212.d

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Roger Babson"
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Robert P. Shuler"
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "William D. Upshaw"
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Claude A. Watson"
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = miscnee.212.a
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.212.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Roger Babson"
			}
		}
		add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.212.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Robert P. Shuler"
			}
		}
		add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.212.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "William D. Upshaw"
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = NEE_new_england_klan_party
			long_name = NEE_new_england_klan_party_long
			ideology = national_populist
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "William D. Upshaw"
			desc = "POLITICS_ROBERT_SHULER_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NEE/Portrait_NEE_William_D_Upshaw.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = klan_nationalism_subtype
			traits = {
				economic_reformer
			}
		}
		add_natpop_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = miscnee.212.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Claude A. Watson"
			}
		}
		add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.1 }
	}
}

			name = "Harry Ault"

			expire = "1.1.1"

		}
	}

		set_country_flag = lermund_student

		limit = {

		}

		}

country_event = {#Ault takes power
	id = lermond.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lermond.3"}
	title = lermond.3.t
	desc = lermond.3.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_ault

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = lermond.3.a #Ault is not that Zased
		add_political_power = -30
		add_tech_bonus = {
				name = industrial_bonus
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = industry
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		random_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
			building = industrial_complex
			size > 0
		include_locked = yes
				}
		OR = {
		is_in_home_area = yes
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				any_owned_state = {
					free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
					}
					is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_BCC
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_FOSTERAULT
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_FOSTERAULT_USA
		}
	}
}

		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
	}
}

country_event = {#New Labor Movement
	id = lermond.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lermond.5"}
	title = lermond.5.t
	desc = lermond.5.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_labor_cooperation

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = lermond.5.a 
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		add_stability = 0.03
		random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = NEE
					is_core_of = NEE
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#Lovell
	id = lermond.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lermond.13"}
	title = lermond.13.t
	desc = lermond.13.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_busy_bees

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = lermond.13.a 
		add_political_power = 50
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = NEE
					is_core_of = NEE
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_BCC
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_HIVE
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_HIVE_USA
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#Industrial society
	id = lermond.15
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lermond.15"}
	title = lermond.15.t
	desc = lermond.15.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_industrial_society

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = lermond.15.a 
		add_political_power = 25
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_2 = yes
		add_tech_bonus = {
				name = industrial_bonus
				bonus = -0.25
				uses = 3
				category = industry
		}
		random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = NEE
					is_controlled_by = NEE
					infrastructure > 0
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_BCC
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ECOANARCHISM
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NEE_lermond_USA
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_ECOANARCHISM_USA
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Join Lermond Faction
	id = lermond.17
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lermond.17"}
	title = lermond.17.t
	desc = lermond.17.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_bcc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

  
	option = { #yes
		name = lermond.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				is_in_faction = no
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT 
		}
	}
	
	option = { #no
		name = lermond.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}
